proto_config, proto_config.is_optional());\n    // null pointer returned only when the filter is optional, then skip all the processes.\n    if (factory == nullptr) {\n      ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Didn't filter_chain_type, is_terminal,\n                                             last_filter_in_current_config);\n    auto filter_config_provider = envoy.filters.network.http_connection_manager]\n\n// [#next-free-field: 62]\nmessage HttpConnectionManager {\n  option (udpa.annotations.versioning).previous_message_type =\n      \"envoy.config.filter.network.http_connection_manager.v2.HttpConnectionManager\";\n\n  enum CodecType {\n    // For every new connection, the connection manager will determine which\n    // codec to use. This mode supports both ALPN for TLS listeners as well as\n    // protocol inference for plaintext listeners. If ALPN data is available, it\n    // is preferred, otherwise protocol inference is used. In almost all cases,\n    // this is the right option to choose for this setting.\n    AUTO = 0;\n\n    // The connection manager will assume that the client is speaking HTTP/1.1.\n    HTTP1 = 1;\n\n    // The connection manager will assume that the client is speaking HTTP/2\n    // (Envoy does not require HTTP/2 to take place over TLS or to use ALPN.\n    // Prior knowledge is allowed).\n    HTTP2 = 2;\n\n    // The connection manager will assume that the client is speaking HTTP/3.\n    // This needs to be consistent with listener and transport socket config.\n    HTTP3 = 3;\n  }\n\n  enum ServerHeaderTransformation {\n    // Overwrite any Server header with the contents of server_name.\n    OVERWRITE = 0;\n\n    // If no Server header is present, append Server server_name\n    // If a Server header is present, pass it through.\n    APPEND_IF_ABSENT = 1;\n\n    // Pass through the value of the server header, and do not append a header\n    // if none is present.\n    PASS_THROUGH = 2;\n  }\n\n  // How to handle the :ref:`config_http_conn_man_headers_x-forwarded-client-cert` (XFCC) HTTP\n  // header.\n  enum ForwardClientCertDetails {\n    // Do not send the XFCC header to the next hop. This is the default value.\n    SANITIZE = 0;\n\n    // When the client connection is mTLS (Mutual TLS), forward the XFCC header\n    // in the request.\n    FORWARD_ONLY = 1;\n\n    // When the client connection is mTLS, append the client certificate\n    // information to the request’s XFCC header and forward it.\n    APPEND_FORWARD = 2;\n\n    // When the client connection is mTLS, reset the XFCC header with the client\n    // certificate information and send it to the next hop.\n    SANITIZE_SET = 3;\n\n    // Always forward the XFCC header in the request, regardless of whether the\n    // client connection is mTLS.","numLines":100,"startLine":1,"totalLines":1401}}}

To do so, we compare the current latest with the *previous* filter. If they\n    37→  // match, then we must be processing a new filter for the first time. We omit this check if we're\n    38→  // the first filter, since the above check handles that case.\n    39→  //\n    40→  // We compare against the previous filter to avoid multiple filter iterations from resetting the\n    41→  // pointer: If we just set latest to current, then the first onData filter iteration would\n    42→  // correctly iterate over the filters and set latest, but on subsequent onData iterations\n    43→  // we'd start from the beginning again, potentially allowing filter N to modify the buffer even\n    44→  // though filter M > N was the filter that inserted data into the buffer.\n    45→  if (current_filter != filters.begin() && latest_filter == std::prev(current_filter)->get()) {\n    46→    latest_filter = current_filter->get();\n    47→  }\n    48→}\n    49→\n    50→} // namespace\n    51→\n    52→void ActiveStreamFilterBase::commonContinue() {\n    53→  if (!canContinue()) {\n    54→    ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"cannot continue filter chain: restoreContextOnContinue(encapsulated_object);\n    64→    state.emplace(&encapsulated_object, parent_.dispatcher_);\n    65→  }\n    66→\n    67→  ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"continuing filter chain: filter={}\", *this,\n    68→                   static_cast<const void*>(this));\n    69→  ASSERT(!canIterate(),\n    70→         \"Attempting to continue iteration while the IterationState is already Continue\");\n    71→  // If iteration has stopped for all frame types, set iterate_from_current_filter_ to true so the\n    72→  // filter iteration starts with the current filter instead of the next one.\n    73→  if (stoppedAll()) {\n    74→    iterate_from_current_filter_ = true;\n    75→  }\n    76→  allowIteration();\n    77→\n    78→  // Only resume with do1xxHeaders() if we've actually seen 1xx headers.\n    79→  if (has1xxHeaders()) {\n    80→    continued_1xx_headers_ = true;\n    81→    do1xxHeaders();\n    82→    // If the response headers have not yet come in, don't continue on with\n    83→    // headers and body. doHeaders expects request headers to exist.\n    84→    if (!parent_.filter_manager_callbacks_.responseHeaders()) {\n    85→      return;\n    86→    }\n    87→ chain registration and execution in Envoy proxy follows a multi-stage flow:\\n\\n## Registration Stage\\n\\n**1. Configuration Definition (Proto)**\\nThe HttpConnectionManager protobuf schema (envoyproxy/envoy api/envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto and envoyproxy/data-plane-api envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto) defines the filter_chain configuration with the http_filters repeated field containing HttpFilter messages. Each HttpFilter has a name, config_type (typed_config or config_discovery), is_optional flag, and disabled flag.\\n\\n**2. Filter Factory Registration (Config Phase)**\\nHttpConnectionManagerConfig (envoyproxy/envoy source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h and .cc) implements the FilterChainFactory interface and is responsible for parsing the HttpConnectionManager configuration. During construction, it uses FilterChainHelper (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h) to process each filter configuration. The FilterChainHelper::processFilters method iterates through the http_filters, validates each filter through the factory registry, and creates FilterFactoryCb callback functions that encapsulate the filter creation logic. These callbacks are stored in filter_factories_ list as FilterFactoryProvider objects.\\n\\n**3. Filter Chain Construction (Connection Creation)**\\nWhen a new HTTP stream is created, FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain (envoyproxy/envoy source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h) is called with a FilterChainManager reference. This method calls FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc) which iterates through the prepared filter factories and invokes each FilterFactoryCb via FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb.\\n\\n## Execution Stage\\n\\n**1. Filter Chain Manager Implementation**\\nFilterChainManager is an interface (envoyproxy/envoy envoy/http/filter_factory.h) that defines how filters are added to the chain through applyFilterFactoryCb method. FilterManager (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.h) implements both FilterChainManager and FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interfaces. When applyFilterFactoryCb is called, it invokes the FilterFactoryCb function passing itself as FilterChainFactoryCallbacks, allowing the factory to call addStreamDecoderFilter and addStreamEncoderFilter to register filters in the chain.\\n\\n**2. Active Filter Wrapping**\\nEach filter added to the chain is wrapped in an ActiveStreamDecoderFilter or ActiveStreamEncoderFilter (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.h) which manages filter state and iteration logic through ActiveStreamFilterBase (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.h). These active wrappers maintain iteration state (Continue, StopSingleIteration, StopAllBuffer, StopAllWatermark) and handle the control flow based on filter callback return values.\\n\\n**3. Runtime Execution**\\nAt runtime, FilterManager maintains two filter chains: decoder filters and encoder filters (stored in std::list containers). When HTTP headers arrive, FilterManager::decodeHeaders iterates through decoder filters in sequence, calling each filter's decodeHeaders method. The return value (FilterHeadersStatus) determines iteration behavior:\\n- FilterHeadersStatus::Continue: Move to next filter\\n- FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration: Stop iteration\\n- FilterHeadersStatus::StopAllIterationAndBuffer: Stop all iteration and buffer data\\n\\nSimilarly, FilterManager::decodeData and FilterManager::decodeTrailers process request body and trailer data. The commonContinue method (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.cc) handles resumption of iteration when filters call continueDecoding().\\n\\nFor response path, FilterManager::encodeHeaders, FilterManager::encodeData, and FilterManager::encodeTrailers process response headers, body, and trailers through registered encoder filters following the same iteration mechanism.\\n\\n**4. Dynamic Configuration (ECDS)**\\nThe system supports dynamic filter configuration through ExtensionConfigDiscoveryService (ECDS). FilterChainHelper can process filters with config_discovery instead of typed_config, creating dynamic filter config providers that can update filter configurations at runtime without requiring proxy reloads.\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n**Configuration-Time vs Runtime-Time Separation:** Filter factory callbacks (FilterFactoryCb) are created once during configuration initialization, then reused for each new stream. This enables efficient filter instantiation.\\n\\n**Visitor Pattern:** FilterChainFactoryCallbacks serves as a visitor interface that filter factories use to add filters to the chain, decoupling filter creation logic from chain construction.\\n\\n**State Machine:** ActiveStreamFilterBase maintains an IterationState enum that tracks whether iteration should continue, stop for single frames, or stop for all frames with optional buffering.\\n\\n**Dual Path Architecture:** The system maintains separate decoder and encoder filter chains to process bidirectional HTTP traffic (request/response), with the router filter serving as the terminal bridge between the two paths.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":169,"cache_read_input_tokens":59441,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":169},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"88dcd5d5-cfeb-4bcb-a621-7bd9d3d2af00","uuid":"e846e8ee-5f4f-47eb-8aac-463468862cdb"}

chain registration and execution in Envoy proxy follows a multi-stage flow:\\n\\n## Registration Stage\\n\\n**1. Configuration Definition (Proto)**\\nThe HttpConnectionManager protobuf schema (envoyproxy/envoy api/envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto and envoyproxy/data-plane-api envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto) defines the filter_chain configuration with the http_filters repeated field containing HttpFilter messages. Each HttpFilter has a name, config_type (typed_config or config_discovery), is_optional flag, and disabled flag.\\n\\n**2. Filter Factory Registration (Config Phase)**\\nHttpConnectionManagerConfig (envoyproxy/envoy source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h and .cc) implements the FilterChainFactory interface and is responsible for parsing the HttpConnectionManager configuration. During construction, it uses FilterChainHelper (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h) to process each filter configuration. The FilterChainHelper::processFilters method iterates through the http_filters, validates each filter through the factory registry, and creates FilterFactoryCb callback functions that encapsulate the filter creation logic. These callbacks are stored in filter_factories_ list as FilterFactoryProvider objects.\\n\\n**3. Filter Chain Construction (Connection Creation)**\\nWhen a new HTTP stream is created, FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain (envoyproxy/envoy source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h) is called with a FilterChainManager reference. This method calls FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc) which iterates through the prepared filter factories and invokes each FilterFactoryCb via FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb.\\n\\n## Execution Stage\\n\\n**1. Filter Chain Manager Implementation**\\nFilterChainManager is an interface (envoyproxy/envoy envoy/http/filter_factory.h) that defines how filters are added to the chain through applyFilterFactoryCb method. FilterManager (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.h) implements both FilterChainManager and FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interfaces. When applyFilterFactoryCb is called, it invokes the FilterFactoryCb function passing itself as FilterChainFactoryCallbacks, allowing the factory to call addStreamDecoderFilter and addStreamEncoderFilter to register filters in the chain.\\n\\n**2. Active Filter Wrapping**\\nEach filter added to the chain is wrapped in an ActiveStreamDecoderFilter or ActiveStreamEncoderFilter (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.h) which manages filter state and iteration logic through ActiveStreamFilterBase (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.h). These active wrappers maintain iteration state (Continue, StopSingleIteration, StopAllBuffer, StopAllWatermark) and handle the control flow based on filter callback return values.\\n\\n**3. Runtime Execution**\\nAt runtime, FilterManager maintains two filter chains: decoder filters and encoder filters (stored in std::list containers). When HTTP headers arrive, FilterManager::decodeHeaders iterates through decoder filters in sequence, calling each filter's decodeHeaders method. The return value (FilterHeadersStatus) determines iteration behavior:\\n- FilterHeadersStatus::Continue: Move to next filter\\n- FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration: Stop iteration\\n- FilterHeadersStatus::StopAllIterationAndBuffer: Stop all iteration and buffer data\\n\\nSimilarly, FilterManager::decodeData and FilterManager::decodeTrailers process request body and trailer data. The commonContinue method (envoyproxy/envoy source/common/http/filter_manager.cc) handles resumption of iteration when filters call continueDecoding().\\n\\nFor response path, FilterManager::encodeHeaders, FilterManager::encodeData, and FilterManager::encodeTrailers process response headers, body, and trailers through registered encoder filters following the same iteration mechanism.\\n\\n**4. Dynamic Configuration (ECDS)**\\nThe system supports dynamic filter configuration through ExtensionConfigDiscoveryService (ECDS). FilterChainHelper can process filters with config_discovery instead of typed_config, creating dynamic filter config providers that can update filter configurations at runtime without requiring proxy reloads.\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n**Configuration-Time vs Runtime-Time Separation:** Filter factory callbacks (FilterFactoryCb) are created once during configuration initialization, then reused for each new stream. This enables efficient filter instantiation.\\n\\n**Visitor Pattern:** FilterChainFactoryCallbacks serves as a visitor interface that filter factories use to add filters to the chain, decoupling filter creation logic from chain construction.\\n\\n**State Machine:** ActiveStreamFilterBase maintains an IterationState enum that tracks whether iteration should continue, stop for single frames, or stop for all frames with optional buffering.\\n\\n**Dual Path Architecture:** The system maintains separate decoder and encoder filter chains to process bidirectional HTTP traffic (request/response), with the router filter serving as the terminal bridge between the two paths.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
